'toh-filter-text',\n  template: '<input type=\"text\" id=\"filterText\" [(ngModel)]=\"filter\" (keyup)=\"filterChanged($event)\" />'\n})\nexport class FilterTextComponent {\n  @Output() changed: EventEmitter<string>;\n  filter: string;\n  constructor() {\n    this.changed = new EventEmitter<string>();\n  }\n  clear() {\n    this.filter = '';\n  }\n  filterChanged(event: any) {\n    event.preventDefault();\n    console.log(`Filter Changed: ${this.filter}`);\n    this.changed.emit(this.filter);\n  }\n}\n\n\n\napp/shared/filter-text/filter-text.service.ts\nimport { Injectable } from '@angular/core';\n@Injectable()\nexport class FilterTextService {\n  constructor() {\n    console.log('Created an instance of FilterTextService');\n  }\n  filter(data: string, props: Array<string>, originalList: Array<any>) {\n    let filteredList: any[];\n    if (data && props && originalList) {\n      data = data.toLowerCase();\n      let filtered = originalList.filter(item => {\n        let match = false;\n        for (let prop of props) {\n          if (item[prop].toString().toLowerCase().indexOf(data) > -1) {\n            match = true;\n            break;\n          }\n        };\n        return match;\n      });\n      filteredList = filtered;\n    } else {\n      filteredList = originalList;\n    }\n    return filteredList;\n  }\n}\n\n\n\napp/heroes/heroes.component.ts\nimport { Component, OnInit } from '@angular/core';\nimport { FilterTextService } from '../shared/filter-text/filter-text.service';\n@Component({\n  moduleId: module.id,\n  selector: 'toh-heroes',\n  templateUrl: 'heroes.component.html'\n})\nexport class HeroesComponent implements OnInit {\n  filteredHeroes: any[] = [];\n  constructor(private filterService: FilterTextService) { }\n  heroes = [\n    { id: 1, name: 'Windstorm' },\n    { id: 2, name: 'Bombasto' },\n    { id: 3, name: 'Magneta' },\n    { id: 4, name: 'Tornado' }\n  ];\n Array<string>, originalList: Array<any>) {\n    let filteredList: any[];\n    if (data && props && originalList) {\n      data = data.toLowerCase();\n      let filtered = originalList.filter(item => {\n        let match = false;\n        for (let prop of props) {\n          if (item[prop].toString().toLowerCase().indexOf(data) > -1) {\n            match = true;\n            break;\n          }\n        };\n        return match;\n      });\n      filteredList = filtered;\n    } else {\n      filteredList = originalList;\n    }\n    return filteredList;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```ts:app/heroes/heroes.component.ts\nimport { Component, OnInit } from '@angular/core';\nimport { FilterTextService } from '../shared/filter-text/filter-text.service';\n@Component({\n  moduleId: module.id,\n  selector: 'toh-heroes',\n  templateUrl: 'heroes.component.html'\n})\nexport class HeroesComponent implements OnInit {\n  filteredHeroes: any[] = [];\n  constructor(private filterService: FilterTextService) { }\n  heroes = [\n    { id: 1, name: 'Windstorm' },\n    { id: 2, name: 'Bombasto' },\n    { id: 3, name: 'Magneta' },\n    { id: 4, name: 'Tornado' }\n  ];\n  filterChanged(searchText: string) {\n    this.filteredHeroes = this.filterService.filter(searchText, ['id', 'name'], this.heroes);\n  }\n  ngOnInit() {\n    this.filteredHeroes = this.heroes;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```html:app/heroes/heroes.component.html\n<div>This is heroes component</div>\n<ul>\n  <li *ngFor=\"let hero of filteredHeroes\">\n    {{hero.name}}\n  </li>\n</ul>\n<toh-filter-text (changed)=\"filterChanged($event)\"></toh-filter-text>\n```\n\n[Back to top](http://qiita.com/Yamamoto0525/items/e59551faf69775a7ad12#%E3%83%88%E3%83%94%E3%83%83%E3%82%AF)\n\n### private spinnerStateChanged: Subscription;\n  constructor(\n    private loggerService: LoggerService,\n    private spinnerService: SpinnerService\n  ) { }\n  ngOnInit() {\n    console.log(this.visible);\n    this.spinnerStateChanged = this.spinnerService.spinnerState\n      .subscribe((state: SpinnerState) => {\n        this.visible = state.show;\n        this.loggerService.log(`visible=${this.visible}`);\n      });\n  }\n  ngOnDestroy() {\n    this.spinnerStateChanged.unsubscribe();\n  }\n}\n```\n\n```html:app/core/spinner/spinner.component.html\n<div 'rxjs/Subject';\nexport interface SpinnerState {\n  show: boolean;\n}\n@Injectable()\nexport class SpinnerService {\n  private spinnerSubject = new Subject<SpinnerState>();\n  spinnerState = this.spinnerSubject.asObservable();\n  constructor() { }\n  show() {\n    this.spinnerSubject.next(<SpinnerState>{ show: true });\n  }\n  hide() {\n    this.spinnerSubject.next(<SpinnerState>{ show: false });\n  }\n}\n```\n\n> app /
